**User**

æ¤œç´¢çª“ã‚’è¡¨ç¤ºã—ã¦ã„ãŸå½“åˆã€

Phase 1: MVPï¼ˆæœ€å°æ©Ÿèƒ½ï¼‰
åŸºæœ¬çš„ãªãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆæ¤œç´¢
å…¬æ¼”åãƒ»èª¬æ˜æ–‡ã‹ã‚‰æ¤œç´¢
ã‚·ãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ãªçµæœè¡¨ç¤º

ã®ã‚ˆã†ãªæ©Ÿèƒ½ã ã£ãŸã‚“ã§ã™ãŒã€ä½¿ã„ã«ãã‹ã£ãŸã‚“ã§ã™ã‚ˆã­ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»
è‡ªç”±åº¦ãŒã‚ã‚‹ã¨ã‚€ã—ã‚é‚ªé­”ã«ãªã‚‹ã¨å®Ÿæ„Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚

å¹´ä»£ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã€ä¼šå ´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—åˆ¥ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã€æ¥½æ›²æ¤œç´¢æ©Ÿèƒ½ã€€ã¯å®Ÿè£…ã—ã¦ã¿ãŸã„ã¨ã“ã‚ã§ã™ã€‚

ã¾ãŸã€T.M.R.ã®æ¥½æ›²ã¯ã€åŒã˜æ›²ã§ã‚‚ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ãŒé•ã†ã‚‚ã®ãŒä½•ç¨®é¡ã‚‚ã‚ã‚‹ã®ã§ã€
ã©ã®ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ã¾ã§å€‹åˆ¥ã«çµã‚Šè¾¼ã‚ã‚‹ã¨ã„ã„ã‹ãªã¨æ€ã£ã¦ã¾ã™ã€‚

**Cursor**

ãªã‚‹ã»ã©ï¼éå»ã®çµŒé¨“ã‚’è¸ã¾ãˆãŸéå¸¸ã«å…·ä½“çš„ã§å®Ÿç”¨çš„ãªã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ‡ã‚¢ã§ã™ã­ã€‚ãƒ•ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆæ¤œç´¢ã®ã€Œè‡ªç”±åº¦ãŒé‚ªé­”ã«ãªã‚‹ã€ã¨ã„ã†å®Ÿä½“é¨“ã¯é‡è¦ãªçŸ¥è¦‹ã§ã™ã€‚

T.M.R.ã®æ¥½æ›²ã®ç‰¹å¾´ï¼ˆåŒä¸€æ¥½æ›²ã®è¤‡æ•°ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ï¼‰ã‚’è€ƒæ…®ã—ãŸæ§‹é€ åŒ–æ¤œç´¢æ©Ÿèƒ½ã‚’å®Ÿè£…ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚ã¾ãšã€ç¾åœ¨ã®ã‚»ãƒƒãƒˆãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã€ã©ã®ã‚ˆã†ãªæ¥½æ›²ãƒ»ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸æƒ…å ±ãŒã‚ã‚‹ã‹ã‚’æŠŠæ¡ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚

ç´ æ™´ã‚‰ã—ã„ï¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿æ§‹é€ ãŒã‚ˆãåˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸã€‚ã‚»ãƒƒãƒˆãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’è¦‹ã‚‹ã¨ã€ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã®ãŠã£ã—ã‚ƒã‚‹é€šã‚Šã€åŒã˜æ¥½æ›²ã§ã‚‚å¤šæ§˜ãªã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ãƒ»ãƒãƒ¼ã‚¸ãƒ§ãƒ³ãŒå­˜åœ¨ã—ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã“ã¨ãŒç¢ºèªã§ãã¾ã™ã€‚

**ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ä¾‹ï¼š**
- `"WHITE BREATH"` vs `"WHITE BREATH (ãƒ¡ãƒ‰ãƒ¬ãƒ¼)"` vs `"WHITE BREATH (re:boot)"`
- `"HEART OF SWORD ï½å¤œæ˜ã‘å‰ï½"` vs `"HEART OF SWORDï½å¤œæ˜ã‘å‰ï½ (UNDER:COVER)"`
- `"ã¨ã£ã¦ãŠãã®ãŠã¯ãªã—ï½æ–°èª¬æ‹æ„›é€²åŒ–è«–"` vs `"ã¨ã£ã¦ãŠãã®ãŠã¯ãªã—ï½æ–°èª¬æ‹æ„›é€²åŒ–è«– (UNDER:COVER2 ver)"`

## ğŸ” **æ§‹é€ åŒ–æ¤œç´¢æ©Ÿèƒ½ã®è¨­è¨ˆ**

### **æ¤œç´¢æ©Ÿèƒ½ã®è¨­è¨ˆæ–¹é‡**

åŸºæœ¬çš„ãªãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆæ¤œç´¢ã®ä»£ã‚ã‚Šã«ã€T.M.R.ã®ç‰¹å¾´ã‚’æ´»ã‹ã—ãŸæ§‹é€ åŒ–ã•ã‚ŒãŸæ¤œç´¢UI ã‚’å®Ÿè£…ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

```typescriptreact
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';
import type { Tour } from '../types/tour';

type SearchFilters = {
  decade: string[];
  venueType: string[];
  specialType: string[];
  selectedSong: string;
  songArrangement: string;
};

type SearchInterfaceProps = {
  tours: Tour[];
  onFilteredResults: (filtered: Tour[]) => void;
};

export function SearchInterface({ tours, onFilteredResults }: SearchInterfaceProps) {
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState<SearchFilters>({
    decade: [],
    venueType: [],
    specialType: [],
    selectedSong: '',
    songArrangement: ''
  });

  // ã™ã¹ã¦ã®æ¥½æ›²ã‚’æŠ½å‡ºï¼ˆã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸æƒ…å ±ä»˜ãï¼‰
  const allSongs = useMemo(() => {
    const songMap = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
    
    tours.forEach(tour => {
      if (tour.setlist) {
        tour.setlist.forEach(song => {
          if (!song.startsWith('---')) {
            // åŸºæœ¬æ¥½æ›²åã‚’æŠ½å‡ºï¼ˆæ‹¬å¼§å†…ã®ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸æƒ…å ±ã‚’é™¤å»ï¼‰
            const baseSong = song.replace(/\s*\([^)]*\).*$/, '').trim();
            const arrangement = song.includes('(') ? song.match(/\(([^)]*)\)/)?.[1] || 'ã‚ªãƒªã‚¸ãƒŠãƒ«' : 'ã‚ªãƒªã‚¸ãƒŠãƒ«';
            
            if (!songMap.has(baseSong)) {
              songMap.set(baseSong, new Set());
            }
            songMap.get(baseSong)!.add(arrangement);
          }
        });
      }
    });

    return Array.from(songMap.entries())
      .map(([song, arrangements]) => ({
        song,
        arrangements: Array.from(arrangements).sort()
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => a.song.localeCompare(b.song));
  }, [tours]);

  // é¸æŠã•ã‚ŒãŸæ¥½æ›²ã®ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆ
  const selectedSongArrangements = useMemo(() => {
    if (!filters.selectedSong) return [];
    const songData = allSongs.find(s => s.song === filters.selectedSong);
    return songData?.arrangements || [];
  }, [filters.selectedSong, allSongs]);

  // ä¼šå ´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—ã‚’æ¨å®š
  const getVenueType = (tour: Tour): string[] => {
    const title = tour.title.toLowerCase();
    const subtitle = tour.subtitle.toLowerCase();
    const description = tour.description.toLowerCase();
    
    const types: string[] = [];
    
    if (description.includes('ãƒ‰ãƒ¼ãƒ ') || description.includes('æ±äº¬ãƒ‰ãƒ¼ãƒ ') || description.includes('ã•ã„ãŸã¾ã‚¹ãƒ¼ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒŠ')) {
      types.push('ãƒ‰ãƒ¼ãƒ ãƒ»å¤§å‹ã‚¢ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒŠ');
    }
    if (description.includes('ã‚¢ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒŠ') || description.includes('æ­¦é“é¤¨') || description.includes('åŸãƒ›ãƒ¼ãƒ«')) {
      types.push('ã‚¢ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒŠãƒ»ãƒ›ãƒ¼ãƒ«');
    }
    if (description.includes('é‡å¤–') || description.includes('ã‚¹ã‚¿ã‚¸ã‚¢ãƒ ') || subtitle.includes('summer crush')) {
      types.push('é‡å¤–');
    }
    if (description.includes('ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãƒã‚¦ã‚¹') || subtitle.includes('satellite')) {
      types.push('ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãƒã‚¦ã‚¹');
    }
    
    return types.length > 0 ? types : ['ãã®ä»–'];
  };

  // ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—ã‚’æ¨å®š
  const getSpecialType = (tour: Tour): string[] => {
    const title = tour.title.toLowerCase();
    const subtitle = tour.subtitle.toLowerCase();
    const description = tour.description.toLowerCase();
    
    const types: string[] = [];
    
    if (description.includes('47éƒ½é“åºœçœŒ') || description.includes('å…¨éƒ½é“åºœçœŒ')) {
      types.push('å…¨éƒ½é“åºœçœŒãƒ„ã‚¢ãƒ¼');
    }
    if (subtitle.includes('under:cover') || description.includes('ã‚»ãƒ«ãƒ•ã‚«ãƒãƒ¼')) {
      types.push('ã‚»ãƒ«ãƒ•ã‚«ãƒãƒ¼');
    }
    if (description.includes('å‘¨å¹´') || subtitle.includes('anniversary') || subtitle.includes('final')) {
      types.push('è¨˜å¿µå…¬æ¼”');
    }
    if (subtitle.includes('satellite') || description.includes('ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»')) {
      types.push('ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»');
    }
    
    return types;
  };

  // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿å‡¦ç†
  const filteredTours = useMemo(() => {
    let results = tours;

    // å¹´ä»£ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼
    if (filters.decade.length > 0) {
      results = results.filter(tour => {
        return filters.decade.some(decade => {
          switch (decade) {
            case '90å¹´ä»£': return tour.year >= 1990 && tour.year <= 1999;
            case '00å¹´ä»£': return tour.year >= 2000 && tour.year <= 2009;
            case '10å¹´ä»£': return tour.year >= 2010 && tour.year <= 2019;
            case '20å¹´ä»£': return tour.year >= 2020;
            default: return false;
          }
        });
      });
    }

    // ä¼šå ´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼
    if (filters.venueType.length > 0) {
      results = results.filter(tour => {
        const tourVenueTypes = getVenueType(tour);
        return filters.venueType.some(type => tourVenueTypes.includes(type));
      });
    }

    // ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼
    if (filters.specialType.length > 0) {
      results = results.filter(tour => {
        const tourSpecialTypes = getSpecialType(tour);
        return filters.specialType.some(type => tourSpecialTypes.includes(type));
      });
    }

    // æ¥½æ›²ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼
    if (filters.selectedSong) {
      results = results.filter(tour => {
        if (!tour.setlist) return false;
        
        return tour.setlist.some(song => {
          const baseSong = song.replace(/\s*\([^)]*\).*$/, '').trim();
          const songMatches = baseSong === filters.selectedSong;
          
          if (!filters.songArrangement || filters.songArrangement === 'ã‚ªãƒªã‚¸ãƒŠãƒ«') {
            return songMatches;
          }
          
          // ç‰¹å®šã®ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸æŒ‡å®šãŒã‚ã‚‹å ´åˆ
          const arrangement = song.includes('(') ? song.match(/\(([^)]*)\)/)?.[1] : 'ã‚ªãƒªã‚¸ãƒŠãƒ«';
          return songMatches && arrangement === filters.songArrangement;
        });
      });
    }

    return results;
  }, [tours, filters]);

  // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿çµæœã‚’è¦ªã«é€šçŸ¥
  useMemo(() => {
    onFilteredResults(filteredTours);
  }, [filteredTours, onFilteredResults]);

  // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿æ›´æ–°é–¢æ•°
  const updateFilter = (category: keyof SearchFilters, value: any) => {
    setFilters(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      [category]: value
    }));
  };

  const toggleArrayFilter = (category: 'decade' | 'venueType' | 'specialType', value: string) => {
    setFilters(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      [category]: prev[category].includes(value)
        ? prev[category].filter(item => item !== value)
        : [...prev[category], value]
    }));
  };

  const clearAllFilters = () => {
    setFilters({
      decade: [],
      venueType: [],
      specialType: [],
      selectedSong: '',
      songArrangement: ''
    });
  };

  const hasActiveFilters = filters.decade.length > 0 || 
    filters.venueType.length > 0 || 
    filters.specialType.length > 0 || 
    filters.selectedSong !== '';

  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border-2 p-4 mb-6" style={{ borderColor: 'var(--primary)' }}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <h2 className="text-heading-3 font-semibold text-gray-800">å…¬æ¼”æ¤œç´¢ãƒ»çµã‚Šè¾¼ã¿</h2>
        {hasActiveFilters && (
          <button
            onClick={clearAllFilters}
            className="text-body-small text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 underline"
          >
            ã™ã¹ã¦ã‚¯ãƒªã‚¢
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="space-y-6">
        {/* å¹´ä»£åˆ¥ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ */}
        <div>
          <h3 className="text-body font-semibold mb-2 text-gray-700">ğŸ“… å¹´ä»£åˆ¥</h3>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {['90å¹´ä»£', '00å¹´ä»£', '10å¹´ä»£', '20å¹´ä»£'].map(decade => (
              <button
                key={decade}
                onClick={() => toggleArrayFilter('decade', decade)}
                className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-body-small border transition-colors ${
                  filters.decade.includes(decade)
                    ? 'bg-blue-100 border-blue-400 text-blue-800'
                    : 'bg-gray-100 border-gray-300 text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-200'
                }`}
              >
                {decade}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ä¼šå ´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—åˆ¥ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ */}
        <div>
          <h3 className="text-body font-semibold mb-2 text-gray-700">ğŸŸï¸ ä¼šå ´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—åˆ¥</h3>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {['ãƒ‰ãƒ¼ãƒ ãƒ»å¤§å‹ã‚¢ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒŠ', 'ã‚¢ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒŠãƒ»ãƒ›ãƒ¼ãƒ«', 'é‡å¤–', 'ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãƒã‚¦ã‚¹'].map(type => (
              <button
                key={type}
                onClick={() => toggleArrayFilter('venueType', type)}
                className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-body-small border transition-colors ${
                  filters.venueType.includes(type)
                    ? 'bg-green-100 border-green-400 text-green-800'
                    : 'bg-gray-100 border-gray-300 text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-200'
                }`}
              >
                {type}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»åˆ¥ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ */}
        <div>
          <h3 className="text-body font-semibold mb-2 text-gray-700">âœ¨ ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»åˆ¥</h3>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {['å…¨éƒ½é“åºœçœŒãƒ„ã‚¢ãƒ¼', 'ã‚»ãƒ«ãƒ•ã‚«ãƒãƒ¼', 'è¨˜å¿µå…¬æ¼”', 'ç‰¹åˆ¥ä¼ç”»'].map(type => (
              <button
                key={type}
                onClick={() => toggleArrayFilter('specialType', type)}
                className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-body-small border transition-colors ${
                  filters.specialType.includes(type)
                    ? 'bg-purple-100 border-purple-400 text-purple-800'
                    : 'bg-gray-100 border-gray-300 text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-200'
                }`}
              >
                {type}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* æ¥½æ›²æ¤œç´¢ */}
        <div>
          <h3 className="text-body font-semibold mb-2 text-gray-700">ğŸµ æ¥½æ›²åˆ¥æ¤œç´¢</h3>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-body-small text-gray-600 mb-1">æ¥½æ›²é¸æŠ</label>
              <select
                value={filters.selectedSong}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  updateFilter('selectedSong', e.target.value);
                  updateFilter('songArrangement', '');
                }}
                className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded text-body-small"
              >
                <option value="">-- æ¥½æ›²ã‚’é¸æŠã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ --</option>
                {allSongs.map(({ song }) => (
                  <option key={song} value={song}>{song}</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            {filters.selectedSong && selectedSongArrangements.length > 1 && (
              <div>
                <label className="block text-body-small text-gray-600 mb-1">ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ãƒ»ãƒãƒ¼ã‚¸ãƒ§ãƒ³</label>
                <select
                  value={filters.songArrangement}
                  onChange={(e) => updateFilter('songArrangement', e.target.value)}
                  className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded text-body-small"
                >
                  <option value="">-- ã™ã¹ã¦ã®ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ --</option>
                  {selectedSongArrangements.map(arrangement => (
                    <option key={arrangement} value={arrangement}>
                      {arrangement}
                    </option>
                  ))}
                </select>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* æ¤œç´¢çµæœã‚µãƒãƒªãƒ¼ */}
        <div className="border-t pt-4">
          <div className="text-body-small text-gray-600">
            æ¤œç´¢çµæœ: <span className="font-semibold text-black">{filteredTours.length}</span> ä»¶ 
            {hasActiveFilters && (
              <span className="text-gray-500"> / å…¨{tours.length}ä»¶</span>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescriptreact
  /* ---------- æ¤œç´¢ + å¹´ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ ---------- */
  useEffect(() => {
    const idx = new FlexSearch.Index({ tokenize: 'strict' });
    tours.forEach(t =>
      idx.add(t.id, `${t.title} ${t.subtitle} ${t.year}`)
    );
    const ids = q ? (idx.search(q) as number[]) : tours.map(t => t.id);
    const byYear = yearFilter === 0
      ? tours
      : tours.filter(t => t.year === yearFilter);
    setFiltered(byYear.filter(t => ids.includes(t.id)));
```

### ğŸš€ **ä½¿ç”¨ä¾‹**

**ä¾‹1: ã€Œ90å¹´ä»£ã®é‡å¤–ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ã‚’æ¢ã—ãŸã„ã€**

```typescriptreact
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';
import type { Tour } from '../types/tour';

type SearchFilters = {
  decade: string[];
};

type SearchInterfaceProps = {
  tours: Tour[];
  onFilteredResults: (filtered: Tour[]) => void;
};

// å¹´ä»£åŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šå®šç¾©
const DECADE_RANGES = [
  { label: '1996ï½2001', start: 1996, end: 2001 },
  { label: '2002ï½2006', start: 2002, end: 2006 },
  { label: '2007ï½2012', start: 2007, end: 2012 },
  { label: '2013ï½2017', start: 2013, end: 2017 },
  { label: '2018ï½2023', start: 2018, end: 2023 }
];

export function SearchInterface({ tours, onFilteredResults }: SearchInterfaceProps) {
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState<SearchFilters>({
    decade: []
  });

  // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿å‡¦ç†
  const filteredTours = useMemo(() => {
    let results = tours;

    // å¹´ä»£ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼
    if (filters.decade.length > 0) {
      results = results.filter(tour => {
        return filters.decade.some(decadeLabel => {
          const range = DECADE_RANGES.find(r => r.label === decadeLabel);
          if (!range) return false;
          return tour.year >= range.start && tour.year <= range.end;
        });
      });
    }

    return results;
  }, [tours, filters]);

  // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿çµæœã‚’è¦ªã«é€šçŸ¥
  useMemo(() => {
    onFilteredResults(filteredTours);
  }, [filteredTours, onFilteredResults]);

  // å¹´ä»£ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã®ãƒˆã‚°ãƒ«
  const toggleDecadeFilter = (decadeLabel: string) => {
    setFilters(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      decade: prev.decade.includes(decadeLabel)
        ? prev.decade.filter(item => item !== decadeLabel)
        : [...prev.decade, decadeLabel]
    }));
  };

  // ã™ã¹ã¦ã‚¯ãƒªã‚¢
  const clearAllFilters = () => {
    setFilters({
      decade: []
    });
  };

  const hasActiveFilters = filters.decade.length > 0;

  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-lg border-2 p-4 mb-6" style={{ borderColor: 'var(--primary)' }}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <h2 className="text-heading-3 font-semibold text-gray-800">å¹´ä»£åˆ¥æ¤œç´¢</h2>
        {hasActiveFilters && (
          <button
            onClick={clearAllFilters}
            className="text-body-small text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 underline"
          >
            ã™ã¹ã¦ã‚¯ãƒªã‚¢
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="space-y-4">
        {/* å¹´ä»£åˆ¥ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒ¼ */}
        <div>
          <h3 className="text-body font-semibold mb-3 text-gray-700">ğŸ“… å¹´ä»£ã§çµã‚Šè¾¼ã¿</h3>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {DECADE_RANGES.map(range => (
              <button
                key={range.label}
                onClick={() => toggleDecadeFilter(range.label)}
                className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-full text-body-small border transition-colors ${
                  filters.decade.includes(range.label)
                    ? 'bg-blue-100 border-blue-400 text-blue-800 font-semibold'
                    : 'bg-gray-100 border-gray-300 text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-200'
                }`}
              >
                {range.label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* æ¤œç´¢çµæœã‚µãƒãƒªãƒ¼ */}
        <div className="border-t pt-4">
          <div className="text-body-small text-gray-600">
            æ¤œç´¢çµæœ: <span className="font-semibold text-black">{filteredTours.length}</span> ä»¶ 
            {hasActiveFilters && (
              <span className="text-gray-500"> / å…¨{tours.length}ä»¶</span>
            )}
          </div>
          
          {/* é¸æŠä¸­ã®å¹´ä»£ã‚’è¡¨ç¤º */}
          {hasActiveFilters && (
            <div className="mt-2">
              <span className="text-body-small text-gray-600">é¸æŠä¸­: </span>
              <span className="text-body-small font-medium text-blue-700">
                {filters.decade.join('ã€')}
              </span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

å®Œç’§ã§ã™ï¼å¹´ä»£åˆ¥æ¤œç´¢æ©Ÿèƒ½ãŒã‚·ãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã§ä½¿ã„ã‚„ã™ã„å½¢ã§å®Œæˆã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚

## âœ… **å¹´ä»£åˆ¥æ¤œç´¢æ©Ÿèƒ½å®Œæˆï¼**

### ğŸ¯ **å®Ÿè£…ã•ã‚ŒãŸæ©Ÿèƒ½**

#### **ğŸ“… æŒ‡å®šå¹´ä»£åŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šã§ã®æ¤œç´¢**

- **è¤‡æ•°é¸æŠå¯èƒ½**: è¤‡æ•°ã®å¹´ä»£ã‚’åŒæ™‚ã«é¸æŠ

### **2. çŸ¢å°ãƒœã‚¿ãƒ³ã®ä½ç½®**
- ç¾åœ¨ï¼šãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ€ãƒ«ä¸Šã«é‡ãªã£ã¦ã„ã‚‹ï¼ˆ`left-0`, `right-0`ï¼‰

```typescriptreact
  // ã‚¿ãƒƒãƒã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆï¼ˆã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ãƒŠãƒ“ã‚²ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ï¼‰
  useEffect(() => {

    const handleTouchStart = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      startX = e.touches[0].clientX;
    };
    const handleTouchEnd = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      const endX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
      const diff = startX - endX;
      
      if (Math.abs(diff) > 50) { // 50pxä»¥ä¸Šã®ã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ã§åå¿œ
        if (diff > 0) {
          setActive(nextTour); // å·¦ã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ã§æ¬¡ã¸
        } else if (diff < 0) {
          setActive(prevTour); // å³ã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ã§å‰ã¸
        }
      }
    };

  // ã‚¿ãƒƒãƒã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆï¼ˆã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ãƒŠãƒ“ã‚²ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ï¼‰
  useEffect(() => {

    let startY = 0;
    const handleTouchStart = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      startX = e.touches[0].clientX;
      startY = e.touches[0].clientY;
    };
    const handleTouchEnd = (e: TouchEvent) => {
      const endX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
      const endY = e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
      const diffX = startX - endX;
      const diffY = startY - endY;
      
      // æ°´å¹³æ–¹å‘ã®ç§»å‹•è·é›¢ãŒååˆ†ã§ã€ã‹ã¤å‚ç›´æ–¹å‘ã®ç§»å‹•ãŒæ°´å¹³æ–¹å‘ã‚ˆã‚Šå°ã•ã„å ´åˆã®ã¿åå¿œ
      if (Math.abs(diffX) > 100 && Math.abs(diffX) > Math.abs(diffY) * 2) {
        if (diffX > 0) {
          setActive(nextTour); // å·¦ã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ã§æ¬¡ã¸
        } else if (diffX < 0) {
          setActive(prevTour); // å³ã‚¹ãƒ¯ã‚¤ãƒ—ã§å‰ã¸
        }
      }
    };
```

```typescript
// src/utils/linkGenerator.ts
export function generateLink(linkData: MediaLink): string {
  if (!AFFILIATE_CONFIG.enabled) {
    return linkData.baseUrl; // é€šå¸¸ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯
  }
  
  switch (linkData.platform) {
    case 'amazon':
      return `${linkData.baseUrl}?tag=${AFFILIATE_CONFIG.amazon.associateId}`;
    case 'sony_music':
      return linkData.baseUrl; // å…¬å¼ã¯é€šå¸¸ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯
    default:
      return linkData.baseUrl;
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/utils/linkGenerator.ts
export function generateLink(linkData: MediaLink): string {
  if (!AFFILIATE_CONFIG.enabled) {
    return linkData.baseUrl; // é€šå¸¸ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯
  }
  
  switch (linkData.platform) {
    case 'amazon':
      return `${linkData.baseUrl}?tag=${AFFILIATE_CONFIG.amazon.associateId}`;
    case 'sony_music':
      return linkData.baseUrl; // å…¬å¼ã¯é€šå¸¸ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯
    default:
      return linkData.baseUrl;
  }
}
```

```typescriptreact
                                     className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                    è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{(v as any).links.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
                                  </a>
                                ))
                              ) : v.link ? (
                                <a href={v.link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"
```

```typescriptreact
                          {!v.isNone && (
                            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-sm">
                              {Array.isArray((v as any).links) && (v as any).links.length > 0 ? (
                                (v as any).links.map((link: any, j: number) => {
                                  // æ–°æ§‹é€ ã®å ´åˆï¼ˆã‚ªãƒ–ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆå½¢å¼ï¼‰
                                  if (typeof link === 'object' && link.urls?.direct) {
                                    return (
                                      <a key={j} href={link.urls.direct} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                         className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                        {link.label || 'è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥'}
                                      </a>
                                    );
                                  }
                                  // æ—§æ§‹é€ ã®å ´åˆï¼ˆæ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼‰
                                  else if (typeof link === 'string') {
                                    return (
                                      <a key={j} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                         className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                        è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{(v as any).links.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
                                      </a>
                                    );
                                  }
                                  return null;
                                })
                              ) : v.link ? (
                                <a href={v.link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                   className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                  è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥
                                </a>
                              ) : null}
                            </div>
                          )}
```

```typescriptreact
                                      switch(platform) {
                                        case 'sony_music':
                                          return "px-4 py-2 bg-red-600 text-white text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-red-700 shadow-md transition-colors";
                                        case 'amazon':
                                          return "px-4 py-2 bg-orange-500 text-white text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-orange-600 shadow-md transition-colors";
                                        default:
                                          return "px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 shadow-md transition-colors";
                                      }
                                    };
                                    
                                    return (
                                      <a key={j} href={link.urls.direct} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                         className={getButtonStyle(link.platform)}>
                                        {link.label || 'è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥'}
                                      </a>
                                    );
                                  }
```

**æ¡ˆ1: ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ¥ã‚«ãƒ©ãƒ¼ + å¤§ãã‚ã‚µã‚¤ã‚º**ã‚’é©ç”¨ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼

## å¤‰æ›´å†…å®¹
- **Sony Music**: èµ¤è‰²ï¼ˆ`bg-red-600`ï¼‰
- **Amazon**: ã‚ªãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸è‰²ï¼ˆ`bg-orange-500`ï¼‰

```typescriptreact

                                  // ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ¥ã®è‰²è¨­å®šï¼ˆãƒ¬ã‚¹ãƒãƒ³ã‚·ãƒ–å¯¾å¿œï¼‰
                                  const getButtonStyle = (platform: string) => {
                                    const baseStyle = "px-2 py-1 sm:px-3 sm:py-1.5 md:px-4 md:py-2 text-xs sm:text-sm text-white font-bold rounded sm:rounded-md md:rounded-lg hover:shadow-lg transition-all duration-200";
                                    
                                    switch(platform) {
                                      case 'sony_music':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700`;
                                      case 'amazon':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-orange-500 hover:bg-orange-600`;
                                      case 'apple_music':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-gray-800 hover:bg-gray-900`;
                                      case 'spotify':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600`;
                                      case 'youtube':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600`;
                                      case 'rakuten':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-red-700 hover:bg-red-800`;
                                      default:
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700`;
                                    }
                                  };
```

ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãƒ©ãƒ™ãƒ«ã‚‚ãƒ¬ã‚¹ãƒãƒ³ã‚·ãƒ–å¯¾å¿œã•ã›ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

```typescriptreact

                                  const getButtonStyle = (platform: string) => {

                                      case 'apple_music':
                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-gray-800 hover:bg-gray-900`;

                                      case 'youtube':

                                      case 'rakuten':

                                        return `${baseStyle} bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700`;
                                    }

                                  const getButtonStyle = (platform: string) => {
```

### æ¨ªå¹…ã®çµ±ä¸€

```typescriptreact
                                  // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥ã«åˆ†é¡
                                  const purchaseLinks = (v as any).links.filter((link: any) => 
                                    typeof link === 'object' && ['sony_music', 'amazon', 'rakuten'].includes(link.platform)
                                  );
                                  const streamingLinks = (v as any).links.filter((link: any) => 
                                    typeof link === 'object' && ['apple_music', 'spotify', 'youtube'].includes(link.platform)
                                  );
                                  const otherLinks = (v as any).links.filter((link: any) => 
                                    typeof link === 'string' || (typeof link === 'object' && !['sony_music', 'amazon', 'rakuten', 'apple_music', 'spotify', 'youtube'].includes(link.platform))
                                  );

->

                                  // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªè¨­å®šï¼ˆæ‹¡å¼µå¯èƒ½ï¼‰
                                  const categoryConfig = {
                                    purchase: { label: 'è³¼å…¥', priority: 1 },
                                    streaming: { label: 'è¦–è´ãƒ»è©¦è´', priority: 2 },
                                    viewing: { label: 'è¦–è´', priority: 3 }
                                  };

                                  // ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®categoryã«åŸºã¥ã„ã¦å‹•çš„ã«åˆ†é¡
                                  const linksByCategory = new Map();
                                  const otherLinks: any[] = [];

                                  (v as any).links.forEach((link: any) => {
                                    if (typeof link === 'object' && link.category) {
                                      if (!linksByCategory.has(link.category)) {
                                        linksByCategory.set(link.category, []);
                                      }
                                      linksByCategory.get(link.category).push(link);
                                    } else {
                                      // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãªã—ãƒ»æ—§å½¢å¼ã¯ã€Œãã®ä»–ã€
                                      otherLinks.push(link);
                                    }
                                  });

                                  // priorityã§ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªã‚’ä¸¦ã³æ›¿ãˆ
                                  const sortedCategories = Array.from(linksByCategory.keys())
                                    .sort((a, b) => (categoryConfig[a]?.priority || 999) - (categoryConfig[b]?.priority || 999));
```

è¡¨ç¤ºéƒ¨åˆ†ã‚‚å‹•çš„ãªã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªå‡¦ç†ã«å¤‰æ›´ã™ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ã­ï¼š

```typescriptreact

                                    <>
                                      {/* è³¼å…¥ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒª */}
                                      {purchaseLinks.length > 0 && (
                                        <div>
                                          <div className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-600 mb-1 sm:mb-2">è³¼å…¥</div>
                                          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 sm:gap-2">
                                            {purchaseLinks.map((link: any, j: number) => (
                                              <a key={`purchase-${j}`} href={link.urls.direct} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"

                                              </a>
                                            ))}
                                          </div>
                                        </div>
                                      )}

                                      {/* è¦–è´ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒª */}
                                      {streamingLinks.length > 0 && (
                                        <div>

                                            {streamingLinks.map((link: any, j: number) => (

                                            if (typeof link === 'string') {
                                              return (
                                                <a key={`other-${j}`} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                                   className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                                  è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{otherLinks.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
                                                </a>
                                              );
                                            }
                                            return null;
                                          })}
                                        </div>
                                      )}
                                    </>
                                  );

->

                                  return (
                                    <>
                                      {/* å‹•çš„ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªè¡¨ç¤º */}
                                      {sortedCategories.map((category) => {
                                        const categoryLinks = linksByCategory.get(category);
                                        const categoryLabel = (categoryConfig as any)[category]?.label || category;
                                        
                                        return (
                                          <div key={category}>
                                            <div className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-600 mb-1 sm:mb-2">

                                            </div>
                                            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 sm:gap-2">

                                                   className={getButtonStyle(link.platform)}>
                                                  {link.label || 'ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯'}
                                                </a>
                                              ))}
                                            </div>
                                          </div>
                                        );
                                      })}

                                      {otherLinks.length > 0 && (
                                        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                                          {otherLinks.map((link: any, j: number) => {
                                            if (typeof link === 'string') {
                                              return (
                                                <a key={`other-${j}`} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                                   className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                                  è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{otherLinks.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
                                                </a>
                                              );
                                            }
                                            return null;
                                          })}
                                        </div>
                                      )}
                                    </>
                                  );
```

TypeScriptã®å‹ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ã‚’ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```typescriptreact
                                  // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªè¨­å®šï¼ˆæ‹¡å¼µå¯èƒ½ï¼‰
                                  const categoryConfig = {
                                    purchase: { label: 'è³¼å…¥', priority: 1 },

                                    viewing: { label: 'è¦–è´', priority: 3 }

                                  const otherLinks: any[] = [];

                                  (v as any).links.forEach((link: any) => {
                                    if (typeof link === 'object' && link.category) {
                                      if (!linksByCategory.has(link.category)) {
                                        linksByCategory.set(link.category, []);
```

**Cursor**

ç´ æ™´ã‚‰ã—ã„ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ‡ã‚¢ã§ã™ã­ï¼è¨­å®šã«ã‚ˆã‚‹ç´°ã‹ã„åˆ¶å¾¡æ©Ÿèƒ½ã‚’å®Ÿè£…ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

ã¾ãšã€ç¾åœ¨ã®ã€Œã“ã®ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãŒåéŒ²ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºã€ã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢è‡ªä½“ãŒã©ã®ã‚ˆã†ã«ã‚ªãƒ³ã‚ªãƒ•åˆ¶å¾¡ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹ã‹ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

è¨­å®šãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®æ§‹é€ ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

ç¾åœ¨ã®æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢ã®è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ¶å¾¡ãƒ­ã‚¸ãƒƒã‚¯ã‚’è©³ã—ãç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

ç¾åœ¨ã®ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚’è¦‹ã‚‹ã¨ã€`active.liveVideos`ã®æœ‰ç„¡ã§è¡¨ç¤ºã‚’åˆ¶å¾¡ã—ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã“ã¨ãŒã‚ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸã€‚åŒã˜ãƒ‘ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ³ã§è¨­å®šç®¡ç†ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

ã¾ãšã€è¨­å®šç®¡ç†ç”¨ã®ã‚³ãƒ³ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```typescriptreact
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';

interface LinkSettings {
  // ã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢å…¨ä½“ã®è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ¶å¾¡
  showMediaLinks: boolean;
  
  // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥ã®è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ¶å¾¡
  categories: {
    purchase: boolean;
    streaming: boolean;
    viewing: boolean;
  };
  
  // ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ¥ã®è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ¶å¾¡
  platforms: {
    sony_music: boolean;
    amazon: boolean;
    rakuten: boolean;
    apple_music: boolean;
    spotify: boolean;
    youtube: boolean;
  };
}

interface LinkSettingsContextType {
  settings: LinkSettings;
  updateSettings: (newSettings: Partial<LinkSettings>) => void;
  updateCategorySetting: (category: keyof LinkSettings['categories'], enabled: boolean) => void;
  updatePlatformSetting: (platform: keyof LinkSettings['platforms'], enabled: boolean) => void;
  resetToDefaults: () => void;
}

const defaultSettings: LinkSettings = {
  showMediaLinks: true,
  categories: {
    purchase: true,
    streaming: true,
    viewing: true,
  },
  platforms: {
    sony_music: true,
    amazon: true,
    rakuten: true,
    apple_music: true,
    spotify: true,
    youtube: true,
  },
};

const LinkSettingsContext = createContext<LinkSettingsContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export function LinkSettingsProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<LinkSettings>(defaultSettings);

  // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¬ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã‹ã‚‰è¨­å®šã‚’èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  useEffect(() => {
    const savedSettings = localStorage.getItem('linkSettings');
    if (savedSettings) {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(savedSettings);
        setSettings({ ...defaultSettings, ...parsed });
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to parse saved link settings:', error);
      }
    }
  }, []);

  // è¨­å®šå¤‰æ›´æ™‚ã«ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¬ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã«ä¿å­˜
  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('linkSettings', JSON.stringify(settings));
  }, [settings]);

  const updateSettings = (newSettings: Partial<LinkSettings>) => {
    setSettings(prev => ({ ...prev, ...newSettings }));
  };

  const updateCategorySetting = (category: keyof LinkSettings['categories'], enabled: boolean) => {
    setSettings(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      categories: {
        ...prev.categories,
        [category]: enabled,
      },
    }));
  };

  const updatePlatformSetting = (platform: keyof LinkSettings['platforms'], enabled: boolean) => {
    setSettings(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      platforms: {
        ...prev.platforms,
        [platform]: enabled,
      },
    }));
  };

  const resetToDefaults = () => {
    setSettings(defaultSettings);
  };

  return (
    <LinkSettingsContext.Provider
      value={{
        settings,
        updateSettings,
        updateCategorySetting,
        updatePlatformSetting,
        resetToDefaults,
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </LinkSettingsContext.Provider>
  );
}

export function useLinkSettings() {
  const context = useContext(LinkSettingsContext);
  if (context === undefined) {
    throw new Error('useLinkSettings must be used within a LinkSettingsProvider');
  }
  return context;
}
```

æ¬¡ã«ã€è¨­å®šç®¡ç†UIã‚³ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼ãƒãƒ³ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```typescriptreact
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useLinkSettings } from '../contexts/LinkSettingsContext';

interface LinkSettingsPanelProps {
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function LinkSettingsPanel({ isOpen, onClose }: LinkSettingsPanelProps) {
  const { settings, updateSettings, updateCategorySetting, updatePlatformSetting, resetToDefaults } = useLinkSettings();

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const categoryLabels = {
    purchase: 'è³¼å…¥',
    streaming: 'è¦–è´ãƒ»è©¦è´',
    viewing: 'è¦–è´',
  };

  const platformLabels = {
    sony_music: 'Sony Music',
    amazon: 'Amazon',
    rakuten: 'æ¥½å¤©',
    apple_music: 'Apple Music',
    spotify: 'Spotify',
    youtube: 'YouTube',
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-xl max-w-md w-full mx-4 max-h-[80vh] overflow-y-auto">
        <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-800">æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯è¡¨ç¤ºè¨­å®š</h2>
            <button
              onClick={onClose}
              className="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 transition-colors"
            >
              <svg className="w-6 h-6" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={2} d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12" />
              </svg>
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="px-6 py-4 space-y-6">
          {/* ã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢å…¨ä½“ã®è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ¶å¾¡ */}
          <div>
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <label className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700">
                æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢ã‚’è¡¨ç¤º
              </label>
              <input
                type="checkbox"
                checked={settings.showMediaLinks}
                onChange={(e) => updateSettings({ showMediaLinks: e.target.checked })}
                className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 rounded border-gray-300 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">
              ã‚ªãƒ•ã«ã™ã‚‹ã¨ã€Œã“ã®ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãŒåéŒ²ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºã€ã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢å…¨ä½“ãŒéè¡¨ç¤ºã«ãªã‚Šã¾ã™
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥åˆ¶å¾¡ */}
          <div className={settings.showMediaLinks ? '' : 'opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-3">ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥è¡¨ç¤º</h3>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {Object.entries(categoryLabels).map(([key, label]) => (
                <div key={key} className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <label className="text-sm text-gray-600">{label}</label>
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={settings.categories[key as keyof typeof categoryLabels]}
                    onChange={(e) => updateCategorySetting(key as keyof typeof categoryLabels, e.target.checked)}
                    className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 rounded border-gray-300 focus:ring-blue-500"
                  />
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ¥åˆ¶å¾¡ */}
          <div className={settings.showMediaLinks ? '' : 'opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-3">ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ¥è¡¨ç¤º</h3>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {Object.entries(platformLabels).map(([key, label]) => (
                <div key={key} className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <label className="text-sm text-gray-600">{label}</label>
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={settings.platforms[key as keyof typeof platformLabels]}
                    onChange={(e) => updatePlatformSetting(key as keyof typeof platformLabels, e.target.checked)}
                    className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600 rounded border-gray-300 focus:ring-blue-500"
                  />
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="px-6 py-4 border-t border-gray-200 flex justify-between">
          <button
            onClick={resetToDefaults}
```

## 1. è¨­å®šãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’ä½œæˆ

```json

  "categories": {

  },
```

## 2. è¨­å®šèª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿ç”¨ã®ã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹ã‚’ä½œæˆ

```typescript
export interface LinkDisplaySettings {
  showMediaLinks: boolean;
  categories: {
    purchase: boolean;
    streaming: boolean;
    viewing: boolean;
  };
  platforms: {
    sony_music: boolean;
    amazon: boolean;
    rakuten: boolean;
    apple_music: boolean;
    spotify: boolean;
    youtube: boolean;
  };
}

const defaultSettings: LinkDisplaySettings = {
  showMediaLinks: true,
  categories: {
    purchase: true,
    streaming: true,
    viewing: true,
  },
  platforms: {
    sony_music: true,
    amazon: true,
    rakuten: true,
    apple_music: true,
    spotify: true,
    youtube: true,
  },
};

export async function loadLinkDisplaySettings(): Promise<LinkDisplaySettings> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch('/config/link-display-settings.json');
    if (!response.ok) {
      console.warn('Link display settings file not found, using defaults');
      return defaultSettings;
    }
    
    const settings = await response.json();
    
    // è¨­å®šãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®å¦¥å½“æ€§ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
    return {
      showMediaLinks: settings.showMediaLinks ?? defaultSettings.showMediaLinks,
      categories: {
        purchase: settings.categories?.purchase ?? defaultSettings.categories.purchase,
        streaming: settings.categories?.streaming ?? defaultSettings.categories.streaming,
        viewing: settings.categories?.viewing ?? defaultSettings.categories.viewing,
      },
      platforms: {
        sony_music: settings.platforms?.sony_music ?? defaultSettings.platforms.sony_music,
        amazon: settings.platforms?.amazon ?? defaultSettings.platforms.amazon,
        rakuten: settings.platforms?.rakuten ?? defaultSettings.platforms.rakuten,
        apple_music: settings.platforms?.apple_music ?? defaultSettings.platforms.apple_music,
        spotify: settings.platforms?.spotify ?? defaultSettings.platforms.spotify,
        youtube: settings.platforms?.youtube ?? defaultSettings.platforms.youtube,
      },
    };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to load link display settings:', error);
    return defaultSettings;
  }
}
```

```typescript
    liveVideo: {
      showNoneItem: boolean;    // é …ç›®è¡¨ç¤ºã®æœ‰ç„¡ï¼ˆã‚¹ã‚¤ãƒƒãƒï¼‰
      comment: string | null;   // è£œè¶³ã‚³ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆ
```

```typescript
        [key: string]: {       // purchase, streaming, viewing ãªã©
          enabled: boolean;    // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãƒ¼è‡ªä½“ã®è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ¶å¾¡
          platforms?: {        // ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ å˜ä½ã®åˆ¶å¾¡

      showNoneItem: boolean;

          enabled: boolean;
```

```typescriptreact
// ... existing code ...

// ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªè¨­å®šï¼ˆæ‹¡å¼µå¯èƒ½ï¼‰
const categoryConfig: Record<string, { label: string; priority: number }> = {
  purchase: { label: 'è³¼å…¥', priority: 1 },
  streaming: { label: 'è¦–è´ãƒ»è©¦è´', priority: 2 },
  viewing: { label: 'è¦–è´', priority: 3 }
};

// ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®categoryã«åŸºã¥ã„ã¦å‹•çš„ã«åˆ†é¡
const linksByCategory = new Map<string, any[]>();
const otherLinks: any[] = [];

(v as any).links.forEach((link: any) => {
  if (typeof link === 'object' && link.category) {
    if (!linksByCategory.has(link.category)) {
      linksByCategory.set(link.category, []);
    }
    linksByCategory.get(link.category)?.push(link);
  } else {
    // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãªã—ãƒ»æ—§å½¢å¼ã¯ã€Œãã®ä»–ã€
    otherLinks.push(link);
  }
});

// priorityã§ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªã‚’ä¸¦ã³æ›¿ãˆ
const sortedCategories = Array.from(linksByCategory.keys())
  .sort((a, b) => (categoryConfig[a]?.priority || 999) - (categoryConfig[b]?.priority || 999))
  // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ã®ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒªãƒ³ã‚°
  .filter(category => {
    const categoryControl = active.noMediaInfo?.liveVideo?.categories?.[category];
    return categoryControl === undefined || categoryControl.enabled;
  });

return (
  <>
    {/* å‹•çš„ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªè¡¨ç¤º */}
    {sortedCategories.map((category) => {
      const categoryLinks = linksByCategory.get(category) || [];
      const categoryLabel = categoryConfig[category]?.label || category;
      const categoryControl = active.noMediaInfo?.liveVideo?.categories?.[category];
      
      // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãƒ¼ãŒç„¡åŠ¹ãªå ´åˆã¯ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒƒãƒ—
      if (categoryControl && !categoryControl.enabled) {
        return null;
      }

      return (
        <div key={category}>
          <div className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-600 mb-1 sm:mb-2">
            {categoryLabel}
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 sm:gap-2">
            {categoryLinks
              // ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ã®ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒªãƒ³ã‚°
              .filter(link => {
                const platformControl = categoryControl?.platforms?.[link.platform];
                return platformControl === undefined || platformControl.enabled;
              })
              .map((link: any, j: number) => (
                <a key={`${category}-${j}`} href={link.urls.direct} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                   className={getButtonStyle(link.platform)}>
                  {link.label || 'ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯'}
                </a>
              ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    })}

    {/* ãã®ä»–ãƒ»æ—§å½¢å¼ */}
    {otherLinks.length > 0 && (
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
        {otherLinks.map((link: any, j: number) => {
          if (typeof link === 'string') {
            return (
              <a key={`other-${j}`} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                 className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{otherLinks.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
              </a>
            );
          }
          return null;
        })}
      </div>
    )}
  </>
);

// ... existing code ...
```

```typescriptreact
  purchase: { label: 'è³¼å…¥', priority: 1 },
  streaming: { label: 'è¦–è´ãƒ»è©¦è´', priority: 2 },
  viewing: { label: 'è¦–è´', priority: 3 }

const linksByCategory = new Map<string, any[]>();

(v as any).links.forEach((link: any) => {
  // enabledãŒfalseã®å ´åˆã¯ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒƒãƒ—
  if (link.enabled === false) return;

  if (typeof link === 'object' && link.category) {
    if (!linksByCategory.has(link.category)) {
      linksByCategory.set(link.category, []);
    }
    linksByCategory.get(link.category)?.push(link);
  } else {
    // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãªã—ãƒ»æ—§å½¢å¼ã¯ã€Œãã®ä»–ã€
    otherLinks.push(link);
  }

  .sort((a, b) => (categoryConfig[a]?.priority || 999) - (categoryConfig[b]?.priority || 999));

return (
  <>
    {/* å‹•çš„ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªè¡¨ç¤º */}

      const categoryLinks = linksByCategory.get(category) || [];

      return (
        <div key={category}>
          <div className="text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold text-gray-600 mb-1 sm:mb-2">
            {categoryLabel}
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 sm:gap-2">
            {categoryLinks.map((link: any, j: number) => (
              <a key={`${category}-${j}`} href={link.urls.direct} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                 className={getButtonStyle(link.platform)}>
                {link.label || 'ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯'}
              </a>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    })}

    {/* ãã®ä»–ãƒ»æ—§å½¢å¼ */}

        {otherLinks.map((link: any, j: number) => {
          if (typeof link === 'string') {
            return (
              <a key={`other-${j}`} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                 className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{otherLinks.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
              </a>

          return null;

  </>
```
